Every 6 months I used to go back on holidays to visit my family and friends back at home. However, since covid hit I've been stuck at home alone with no friends or even family for almost 9 months now, and it's most likely still going to be that way for another 5 months. The sheer boredom from loneliness and unable to do anything with anyone has taken a major toll on my physical and mental health. I feel alone and sad all the time.
